%%
77
newds.SelectedVariableNames = newds.VariableNames;
78
preview(newds)
79
%% close all open files
80
fclose('all');
81
%% write to txt files w.r.t. unique KNX group addrs
82
83
%create dir for files
84
[SUCCESS,MESSAGE,MESSAGEID] = mkdir(base_dir,'KNXfiles');

display(['Creating dir result: ' num2str(SUCCESS)]);
86
display(['MESSAGE: ' num2str(MESSAGE)]);
87
display(['MESSAGEID: ' num2str(MESSAGEID)]);
88
89
destination = [base_dir,'KNXfiles'];
90
oldname = 'combined.txt';

for i = 1:length(D.Value{1})

## Specify the system equations
8

)/Ce * dt +
9
exp(s11) * dw1)
10
model$addSystem(dTf ~ ( UAf*(Ti - Tf) + Qfh )/Cf * dt +
11
exp(s22) * dw2)
12

UAe*(Te -Ti) + UAf*(Tf - Ti) + Aw*PsiS)/Ca * dt +
13
exp(s33) * dw3)
14

kfh*5.555556e-05*mf
15
exp(s44) * dw4)

Predictive Kalman Filter
Scripts for Predictive Kalman Filter.
1
function [P,Re,Kpx] = PKFDesign(Model)
2
% stationary Predictive Kalman Filter
3
4
A = Model.Ad;
5
C = Model.Cd;
6
G = Model.G; % process disturbance model
7
8
Rww = Model.Rww;% process noise covariance
9
Rwv = Model.Rwv;% cross covariance between process and measurement noise
10
Rvv = Model.Rvv;% measurement noise covariance
11
12
% state estimate covariance
13
P = dare(A',C',G*Rww*G', Rvv,G*Rwv);
14
% innovation covariance
15
Re = C*P*C' + Rvv;
16
% kalman gains
17
Kpx = (A*P*C' + G*Rwv)/Re;
18
19
end
1
function [Zhat] = PKFPredict(MPC,xhatp,Uk_tilde,Dk_tilde)
2
% xhatp - xhat_k|k-1
3
%
Uk_tilde
- optimized input sequence or guess of it
4
% Dk_tilde - disturbance forecast for k=1,2,...,N
5
6
Zhat = MPC.Phix*xhatp + MPC.Gamma_u_t*Uk_tilde + MPC.Gamma_d_t*Dk_tilde;
7
end

function [xhatp] = PKFCompute(Model,xhat, up,yp, dp )
2
% Predictive Kalman Filter
3
4
% INPUTS:
5
% xhat - previous state estimate, xhat_k-1|k-2
6
% up - previous input; uhat_k-1|k-2 = uk-1
7
% dp - previous disturbance; dhat_k-1|k-2
8
% Model - struct
9
10
% OUTPUTS:
11
% xhatp - predicted state; xhat_k|k-1
12
13
A = Model.Ad;
14
C = Model.Cd;
==PAGE:227==
SMART START
205
15
Bu = Model.Bu;
16
Bd = Model.Bd;
17
Du = Model.Du;
18
Dd = Model.Dd;
19
Kpx = Model.Kpx;
20
21
% predicted output
22
yhat = C*xhat + Du*up + Dd*dp;%yk-1|k-2
23
24
ek = yp - yhat;% innovation
25
xhatp = A*xhat + Bu*up + Bd*dp + Kpx*ek;% predicted state

function [N,f,intcon,A,b,Aeq,beq,lb,ub] = formSchedulingProblem(prices,...
2
power,STi,u_m1,T_ONmin,Del_flex,Del_overall)
3
4
% author: Jakub Krzysztof Rodek
5
% date : 28-03-2017
6
7
%name : formSchedulingProblem
8
9
%description: the function to create problem of scheduling appliances with
10
%subtasks
11
12
% input arguments:
13
% prices - electricity price vector
14
% power - power consumption level for tasks within an event; it is const
15
% for a task
16
% STi - number of tasks
17
% u_m1 - previous ON status of appliances; a vector
18
% T_ON - minimum ON time of appliances
19
% Del_flex - delay flexibilities of appliances; how long can be the delay
==PAGE:232==
210
FOURTH APPENDIX
20
% between Start command from a user until the actual power-up of an
21
% appliance
22
23
% output arguments:
24
% f,intcon,A,b,Aeq,beq,lb,ub - parameters for the function intlinprog
25
% N - Prediction horizon; it changes because at any given point we use
26
% information about electricity prices and that info has limited time span;
27
% N belongs to [12;36]
28
29
30
%% objective function
31
32
[nr,nc] = size(prices);
33
N = max(nr,nc);% N - Prediction horizon
34
35
if(nr > nc)
36
prices = prices'; % converting to a row vector
37
end
38
39
[nr,nc] = size(power);
40
if(nc > nr)
41
power = power'; % converting to a column vector
42
end
43
44
Prices = repmat(prices,STi,1); % prices grid
45
46
Power = repmat(power,1,N); % power grid
47
48
f1 = Power.*Prices;%all(f1 == Prices.*Power) = 1
49
50
F = f1(:);
51
52
f = [F;zeros(2*STi*N,1)]; % zeros for the z and y part of vector
53
% E = [u^T,z^T,y^T]^T; ; min f'*E
54
55
%% equality constraints:
56
%% constraint 1 - u_tau - u_tau-1 = z_tau - y_tau
57
58
lambda1 = eye(N)-[zeros(1,N); eye(N-1) zeros(N-1,1)];
59
lambda = kron(lambda1,eye(STi));
60
tem = [lambda kron(-eye(N),eye(STi)) kron(eye(N),eye(STi))];
61
62
% O_-1 component
63
comp2 = zeros(N*STi,1);
64
comp2(1:STi) = u_m1;% u_m1 - on/off status from the previous optimization
65
66
%% constraint 2 - sum(z) = 1 && sum(y) = 1
67
L1 = kron(ones(1,N),eye(STi));
68
Z1 = zeros(STi,STi*N);
69
70
%% putting it all together
71
72
Aeq = [tem; Z1 L1 Z1; Z1 Z1 L1];
73
beq = [comp2;ones(2*STi,1)];
74
% finished equality constraints
75
%###################################################
76
%% inequality constraints:
==PAGE:233==
SMART START
211
77
% z <= u
78
% components [u z y]
79
c1 = [kron(eye(N),-eye(STi)) kron(eye(N),eye(STi)) zeros(STi*N)];
80
b1 = zeros(STi*N,1);
81
82
%y <= 1 - u
83
c2 = [kron(eye(N),eye(STi)) zeros(STi*N) kron(eye(N),eye(STi))];
84
b2 = ones(STi*N,1);
85
86
%% constraint 4th - min operating time
87
88
Z = zeros(STi*N);
89
for tau = 1:N % tau = 0 ... N-1
90
for task = 1:STi % task number
91
indc = (STi*(max(1,tau - T_ONmin(task) + 1) - 1) + task) : STi :...
92
(STi*(tau - 1) + task);
93
indr = task + STi*(tau - 1);
94
Z(indr , indc) = 1;
95
end
96
end
97
98
99
U = -eye(STi*N);
100
101
Y = zeros(STi*N);
102
103
c3 = [U, Z,Y];
104
b3 = zeros(STi*N,1);
105
106
%% operation dependence constraints
107
108
[P_pi] = permutationMat(N,STi); % P_pi - permutation matrix
109
temp1 = 0:N-1; % tau
110
temp2 = zeros(1,N);
111
112
